## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / nonlinear oscillators
**Analysis**: This task involves finding the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position, velocity, and time. The equation of motion for such systems typically involves restoring forces (functions of x), damping terms (functions of v), and possibly driving forces (functions of t).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple restoring force proportional to displacement)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (restoring force plus linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Duffing with damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring force plus damping)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (forced nonlinear oscillator)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - x**2) * v (nonlinear damping dependent on position)
- Quadratic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (asymmetric restoring force)
- Cubic-quintic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order nonlinear restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity damping)
- Pendulum-like: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (sinusoidal restoring force approximating a pendulum)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (Rayleigh-type nonlinear damping)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * cos(c1 * t) (time-modulated restoring force)
- Mixed nonlinear: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x * v**2 (position-velocity coupling)
- General polynomial restoring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 + c3 * v (polynomial restoring force with damping)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) ŌåÆ symmetric potential wells preserving oscillation symmetry
- Position-dependent damping terms like (1 - x**2)*v ŌåÆ self-sustained oscillations (limit cycles)
- Cubic restoring force x**3 ŌåÆ hardening or softening spring behavior depending on sign
- Sinusoidal functions of position sin(c*x) ŌåÆ pendulum-like or periodic potential dynamics
- Velocity-squared or velocity-cubed terms ŌåÆ nonlinear dissipation or energy-dependent damping
- Cosine/sine functions of time ŌåÆ external periodic driving forces
- Products of position and velocity (x*v) ŌåÆ non-conservative coupling or gyroscopic-like terms
- Even powers of x in restoring force (x**2) ŌåÆ broken symmetry and drift in oscillation center
- Absence of explicit time dependence ŌåÆ autonomous/conservative system structure
- Parametric terms x*cos(c*t) ŌåÆ parametric resonance and instability phenomena
